class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">\n     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n    </div>\n    <div id="contentSub">\n    </div>\n    <div the tropical cyclone in 2011.  <tr style="display:none">\n        <td colspan="2">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding:0px 2px;white-space:nowrap">\n         Fatalities\n       )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding:0px 2px;white-space:nowrap">\n         Areas affected\n        </th>\n        <td style="padding:0px 2px">\n         <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n          Hispaniola\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n          Lesser Antilles\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Greater_Antilles" title="Greater Antilles">\n          Greater Antilles\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos" title="Turks and Caicos">\n          Turks and Caicos\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">\n          Bahamas\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n          East Coast of the United States\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n          Vermont\n         </a>\n         <small>\n          (\n          <a href="/wiki/Landfall" title="Landfall">\n           Landfalls\n          </a>\n          in\n          <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n           North Carolina\n          </a>\n          ,\n          <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n           New Jersey\n          </a>\n          ,\n          <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n           New York\n          </a>\n         </small>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Canada" title="Atlantic Canada">\n          Atlantic Canada\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;padding:0px 2px">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center; border-top:#aaa 1px solid;">\n         Part of the\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n           2011 Atlantic hurricane season\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr style="display:none">\n        <td colspan="2">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Hurricane Irene\n       </b>\n       was a large and destructive\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       which affected much of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        East Coast of the United States\n       </a>\n       during late August 2011. Irene is ranked as the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_costliest_Atlantic_hurricanes" title="List of costliest Atlantic hurricanes">\n        ninth-costliest hurricane\n       </a>\n       in United States history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The ninth\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        named storm\n       </a>\n       , first hurricane, and first major hurricane of the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2011 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       , Irene originated from a well-defined\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">\n        Atlantic\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       that began showing signs of organization east of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       . Due to development of\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">\n        atmospheric convection\n       </a>\n       and a closed center of circulation, the system was designated as Tropical Storm Irene on August\xc2\xa020, 2011. After intensifying, Irene made\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landfall_(meteorology)" title="Landfall (meteorology)">\n        landfall\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Croix" title="St. Croix">\n        St. Croix\n       </a>\n       as a strong tropical storm later that day. Early on August\xc2\xa021, the storm made a second landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       . While crossing the island, Irene strengthened into a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Category_1_hurricane" title="Category 1 hurricane">\n        Category 1 hurricane\n       </a>\n       . The storm paralleled offshore of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       , continuing to slowly intensify in the process. Shortly before making four landfalls in the Bahamas, Irene peaked as a 120\xc2\xa0mph (190\xc2\xa0km/h) Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Thereafter, the storm slowly leveled off in intensity as it struck the Bahamas and then curved northward after passing east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Bahama" title="Grand Bahama">\n        Grand Bahama\n       </a>\n       . Continuing to weaken, Irene was downgraded to a Category\xc2\xa01 hurricane before making landfall on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa027, becoming the first hurricane to make landfall in the United States since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">\n        Hurricane Ike\n       </a>\n       in 2008. Early on the following day, the storm re-emerged into the Atlantic from southeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       . Although Irene remained a hurricane over water, it weakened to a tropical storm while making yet another landfall in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Little_Egg_Inlet" title="Little Egg Inlet">\n        Little Egg Inlet\n       </a>\n       in southeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa027. A few hours later, Irene made its ninth and final landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Brooklyn" title="Brooklyn">\n        Brooklyn\n       </a>\n       , New York City. Early on August\xc2\xa029, Irene transitioned into an extratropical cyclone hitting\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </a>\n       after remaining inland as a tropical cyclone for less than 12\xc2\xa0hours.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Throughout its path, Irene caused widespread destruction and at least 56 deaths. Damage estimates throughout the United States are estimated near $15.6 billion,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which made it the ninth-costliest hurricane in United States history, only behind\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Andrew" title="Hurricane Andrew">\n        Hurricane Andrew\n       </a>\n       of 1992,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ivan" title="Hurricane Ivan">\n        Hurricane Ivan\n       </a>\n       of 2004, Hurricanes\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Wilma" title="Hurricane Wilma">\n        Wilma\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Katrina\n       </a>\n       of 2005,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">\n        Hurricane Ike\n       </a>\n       of 2008,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy" title="Hurricane Sandy">\n        Hurricane Sandy\n       </a>\n       in 2012, and Hurricanes\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Harvey\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Irma\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">\n        Maria\n       </a>\n       in 2017. In addition, monetary losses in the Caribbean and Canada were $830\xc2\xa0million and $130\xc2\xa0million respectively for a total of nearly $16.6 billion in damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-csr-damagetotal_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-csr-damagetotal-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#Meteorological_history">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           1\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Meteorological history\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2">\n         <a href="#Preparations">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           2\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Preparations\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-3">\n           <a href="#Caribbean">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Caribbean\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n           <a href="#United_States">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-5">\n             <a href="#Southeast">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               2.2.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Southeast\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-6">\n             <a href="#Mid-Atlantic">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               2.2.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Mid-Atlantic\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-7">\n             <a href="#New_England">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               2.2.3\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               New England\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-8">\n           <a href="#Canada">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Canada\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-9">\n         <a href="#Impact">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Impact\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-10">\n           <a href="#Lesser_Antilles">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Lesser Antilles\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-11">\n           <a href="#Greater_Antilles">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Greater Antilles\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-12">\n             <a href="#Puerto_Rico">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.2.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Puerto Rico\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-13">\n             <a href="#Hispaniola">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.2.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Hispaniola\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-14">\n             <a href="#Cuba">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.2.3\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Cuba\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15">\n           <a href="#Turks_and_Caicos_and_the_Bahamas">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Turks and Caicos and the Bahamas\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-16">\n           <a href="#United_States_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             United States\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-17">\n             <a href="#Southeast_2">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.4.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Southeast\n              </span>\n             </a>\n             <ul>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-18">\n               <a href="#Florida">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.1.1\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Florida\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-19">\n               <a href="#South_Carolina">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.1.2\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 South Carolina\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-20">\n               <a href="#North_Carolina">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.1.3\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 North Carolina\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-21">\n               <a href="#Virginia">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.1.4\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Virginia\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n             </ul>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-22">\n             <a href="#Mid-Atlantic_states">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.4.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Mid-Atlantic states\n              </span>\n             </a>\n             <ul>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-23">\n               <a href="#Maryland">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.2.1\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Maryland\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-24">\n               <a href="#Delaware">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.2.2\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Delaware\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-25">\n               <a href="#Pennsylvania">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.2.3\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Pennsylvania\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-26">\n               <a href="#New_Jersey">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.2.4\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 New Jersey\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-27">\n               <a href="#New_York">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.2.5\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 New York\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n             </ul>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-28">\n             <a href="#New_England_2">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               3.4.3\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               New England\n              </span>\n             </a>\n             <ul>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-29">\n               <a href="#Connecticut">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.3.1\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Connecticut\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-30">\n               <a href="#Massachusetts">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.3.2\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Massachusetts\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-31">\n               <a href="#Rhode_Island">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.3.3\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Rhode Island\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n              <li class="toclevel-4 tocsection-32">\n               <a href="#Vermont">\n                <span class="tocnumber">\n                 3.4.3.4\n                </span>\n                <span class="toctext">\n                 Vermont\n                </span>\n               </a>\n              </li>\n             </ul>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33">\n           <a href="#Maine">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.5\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Maine\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-34">\n           <a href="#Canada_2">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.6\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Canada\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-35">\n         <a href="#Retirement">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Retirement\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-36">\n         <a href="#See_also">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           See also\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-37">\n         <a href="#Notes">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           6\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Notes\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-38">\n         <a href="#References">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           7\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           References\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-39">\n         <a href="#External_links">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           8\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           External links\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Meteorological_history">\n        Meteorological history\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Meteorological history">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_track.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="1024" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Irene_2011_track.png/220px-Irene_2011_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Irene_2011_track.png/330px-Irene_2011_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Irene_2011_track.png/440px-Irene_2011_track.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_track.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map plotting the track and intensity of the storm, according to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n          Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On August 15, 2011, a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       exited the west African coast, and emerged into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">\n        Atlantic\n       </a>\n       , characterized by distinct low-level\n       <a href="/wiki/Cyclonic_rotation" title="Cyclonic rotation">\n        cyclonic rotation\n       </a>\n       and deep tropical humidity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twd-2p-15_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twd-2p-15-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It remained well-defined while moving steadily westward for several days to the south of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">\n        Cape Verde Islands\n       </a>\n       , although at the time any notable\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">\n        convection\n       </a>\n       occurred well to the southwest of its axis.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twd-2p-16_7-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twd-2p-16-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the wave distanced itself from the islands, development of thunderstorms and showers in its proximity continued to remain scarce, and it became rather broad in appearance.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gtwo-2a-18_8-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-gtwo-2a-18-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 19, the convective structure began to show signs of organization as the associated\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_pressure" title="Atmospheric pressure">\n        atmospheric pressure\n       </a>\n       lowered, and with a progressively favorable environment situated ahead of the wave its chances of undergoing\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclogenesis" title="Tropical cyclogenesis">\n        tropical cyclogenesis\n       </a>\n       markedly increased.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twd-8a-19_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twd-8a-19-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gtwo-8a-20_10-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-gtwo-8a-20-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The strong thunderstorm activity continued to become more pronounced around the main\n       <a href="/wiki/Low-pressure_area" title="Low-pressure area">\n        low-pressure feature\n       </a>\n       . By August 20, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       noted that\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       formation was imminent as the wave neared the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gtwo-2p-20_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-gtwo-2p-20-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hunters" title="Hurricane Hunters">\n        reconnaissance aircraft\n       </a>\n       confirmed the presence of a small surface circulation center just southwest of a burst of vigorous convection and unusually high\n       <a href="/wiki/Maximum_sustained_wind" title="Maximum sustained wind">\n        sustained winds\n       </a>\n       , indicating sufficient organization for the cyclone to be upgraded into Tropical Storm Irene at 23:00\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-7p-20_12-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-7p-20-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Irene was positioned about 190\xc2\xa0mi (310\xc2\xa0km) east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       when it was classified and named, along weakening\n       <a href="/wiki/High-pressure_area" title="High-pressure area">\n        high pressure\n       </a>\n       over the west-central Atlantic, inducing a roughly west-northwestward path for most of its journey through the eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-7p-20_12-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-7p-20-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Its mid-level circulation continued to become better established as hints of pronounced\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">\n        banding features\n       </a>\n       curved north of the surface center.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-11p-20_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-11p-20-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 21, the surface center reformed closer to the deepest convection; furthermore, an\n       <a href="/wiki/Anticyclone" title="Anticyclone">\n        anticyclone\n       </a>\n       aloft provided supportive\n       <a href="/wiki/Outflow_(meteorology)" title="Outflow (meteorology)">\n        outflow\n       </a>\n       over the cyclone. With the improved structure, as well as light\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       and high\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       , Irene was forecast to strengthen to near hurricane force prior to landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5a-21_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5a-21-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-11a-21_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-11a-21-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over the subsequent day (August 22), while passing near the island of\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Croix,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Croix, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint Croix\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        U.S. Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ipa-8p-21_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ipa-8p-21-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Irene traced toward\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       , more northward than initially expected, where it underwent a considerable increase in strength and organization.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-11p-21_17-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-11p-21-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hours later, Irene moved ashore, approaching from the southeast at landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Cayo_Santiago" title="Cayo Santiago">\n        Punta Santiago\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Humacao,_Puerto_Rico" title="Humacao, Puerto Rico">\n        Humacao, Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       , with estimated sustained winds of 70\xc2\xa0mph (110\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcu-130a-22_18-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcu-130a-22-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite the storm\'s interaction with land,\n       <a href="/wiki/Weather_radar" title="Weather radar">\n        radar imagery\n       </a>\n       showed a ragged\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       -like feature, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Weather_radar#Velocity" title="Weather radar">\n        Doppler weather radar data\n       </a>\n       indicated wind speeds in excess of\n       <a href="/wiki/Beaufort_scale" title="Beaufort scale">\n        hurricane force\n       </a>\n       . Just after its initial landfall, Irene was accordingly upgraded to a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Category_1_hurricane" title="Category 1 hurricane">\n        Category 1 hurricane\n       </a>\n       , the first of the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2011 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5a-22_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5a-22-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_2" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:384px"&gt;&lt;video
