data-title="Small WebM (240P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 240P" data-transcodekey="240p.webm" data-width="320" data-height="240" data-bandwidth="253664" data-framerate="15"/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\'>\n         <img alt="File:Irene goe 201108 h264 sm xo.ogv" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Irene_goe_201108_h264_sm_xo.ogv/220px--Irene_goe_201108_h264_sm_xo.ogv.jpg" style="width:220px;height:165px"/>\n         <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/5d/Irene_goe_201108_h264_sm_xo.ogv" target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irene_goe_201108_h264_sm_xo.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Loop showing Irene\'s progress as viewed from the\n         <a href="/wiki/GOES_13" title="GOES 13">\n          GOES-EAST\n         </a>\n         satellite\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       With the hurricane then situated just north of the mountainous coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       , the storm deepened little after reemerging over water, and any additional organization during the rest of the day was gradual.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5p-22_20-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5p-22-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-11p-22_21-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-11p-22-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After briefly weakening on August 23,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5p-23_22-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5p-23-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       however, Irene began to develop a distinct eye encircled by an area of deepening convection the next morning. Moving erratically through the southeast\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Bahamas" title="The Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </a>\n       over very warm waters,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5a-24_23-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5a-24-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Irene quickly expanded as its outflow aloft became very well established; the cyclone intensified into a Category 3\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_scales#Atlantic_and_East_Pacific" title="Tropical cyclone scales">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       as it recurved toward the northwest along a weakness in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Subtropical_ridge" title="Subtropical ridge">\n        subtropical ridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-id-5p-24_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-id-5p-24-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone subsequently underwent a partial\n       <a href="/wiki/Eyewall_replacement_cycle" title="Eyewall replacement cycle">\n        eyewall replacement cycle\n       </a>\n       , which resulted in some reduction in its winds. Although a distinct eye redeveloped for a few hours, it obscured once again soon thereafter; Irene was unable to recover from the cycle, with no further significant intensification expected thereafter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2656" data-file-width="4080" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg/240px-Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg/360px-Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg/480px-Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg 2x" width="240"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene%27s_demise.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Irene\'s remnants on August 30, in the process of being absorbed by another system.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Early on August 27, Irene further weakened to a Category 1 hurricane as it approached the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At 7:30\xc2\xa0am EDT (11:30 UTC) the same day, Irene made landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Lookout_(North_Carolina)" title="Cape Lookout (North Carolina)">\n        Cape Lookout\n       </a>\n       , on North Carolina\'s Outer Banks, with winds of 85\xc2\xa0mph (137\xc2\xa0km/h), but exhibited an unusually low pressure of 951 mbar, which is typically found in a category 3 hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After having tracked over land for about 10 hours, the eye of Irene became cloud-filled, although the center remained well-defined on radar images.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early in the evening of August 27, Irene re-emerged into the Atlantic near the southern end of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       as a marginal Category 1 hurricane, slowly weakening as it continued northward and weakening to a tropical storm early on August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis30A_29-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis30A-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Shortly before sunrise, at 5:35\xc2\xa0am EDT (0935 UTC) on August 28, Irene made a second landfall at\n       <a href="/wiki/Brigantine,_New_Jersey" title="Brigantine, New Jersey">\n        Brigantine\n       </a>\n       in southeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       with winds of 70\xc2\xa0mph (110\xc2\xa0km/h)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nhc_30-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nhc-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and soon after moved over water again, hugging the New Jersey coastline. About 3 1/2 hours later, Tropical Storm Irene made landfall with 65\xc2\xa0mph (105\xc2\xa0km/h) winds in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Coney_Island" title="Coney Island">\n        Coney Island\n       </a>\n       neighborhood of\n       <a href="/wiki/Brooklyn" title="Brooklyn">\n        Brooklyn\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Following its final New York landfall, Irene moved northeast over\n       <a href="/wiki/New_England" title="New England">\n        New England\n       </a>\n       while maintaining its strength, before it was declared an extratropical cyclone early on August 29, while its center was located near the New Hampshire/Vermont border.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During that day, the system continued to move towards the northeast, before it was absorbed by a frontal system early on August 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">\n        Preparations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Preparations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Caribbean">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In response to the formation of Irene,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        tropical storm warnings\n       </a>\n       were issued for all of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">\n        Leeward Islands\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Also in the Lesser Antilles, the storm\'s approach prompted authorities in the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">\n        U.S. Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       to close off air- and seaports, as well as to open public shelters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vidn_32-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-vidn-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As Irene was forecast to make landfall on\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       , a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches#Tropical_Storm_Watch" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        tropical storm watch\n       </a>\n       was initially issued for the south coast of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       , though it was upgraded to a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches#Hurricane_Warning" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        hurricane warning\n       </a>\n       on August 21, after strengthening was forecast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In light of the expected intensification to hurricane status, a tropical storm warning was also issued for the northern coast fire of that country, while a tropical storm watch was put in effect for all of\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       ; the tropical storm warning for Puerto Rico was simultaneously upgraded to a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Watch" title="Hurricane Watch">\n        hurricane watch\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that day, all of the Dominican Republic was placed under a hurricane warning, with the tropical storm watch for Haiti upgraded to a warning and a tropical storm watch initiated for the southeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Bahamas" title="The Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">\n        Turks and Caicos Islands\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As Irene\'s forecast track became justified, the latter watch was upgraded to a warning on August 22, while a hurricane watch was declared for the central Bahamas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">\n        United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       With Irene\'s projected path fixed over much of the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        United States East Coast\n       </a>\n       , over 65 million people from the Carolinas to northern New England were estimated to be at risk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to the threat, state officials, as well as utilities, transportation facilities, ports, industries, oil refineries, and nuclear power plants, promptly prepared to activate emergency plans; residents in the areas stocked up on food supplies and worked to secure homes, vehicles and boats.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       States of emergency and hurricane warnings were declared for much of the East Coast, including\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washpost26_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washpost26-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland" title="Maryland">\n        Maryland\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washpost26_40-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washpost26-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-do_41-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-do-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        District of Columbia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dc-emergency_42-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-dc-emergency-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-abc27_43-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-abc27-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjblog_44-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjblog-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island" title="Rhode Island">\n        Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rigov_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-rigov-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wcax_47-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wcax-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire" title="New Hampshire">\n        New Hampshire\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnliveblog_48-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnliveblog-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mueller_49-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mueller-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In advance of the storm, hundreds of thousands of people evacuated near coastal areas, and hundreds of shelters were prepared. Many gasoline stations in the region reported shortages due to the preparations for Irene.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gasshortage_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-gasshortage-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Six\n       <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">\n        Major League Baseball\n       </a>\n       games were postponed or moved to August 27 in doubleheaders, and one\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">\n        National Football League\n       </a>\n       preseason game was postponed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Giants_53-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Giants-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Barclays" title="The Barclays">\n        The Barclays\n       </a>\n       golf tournament was shortened\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-transithalt_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-transithalt-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and three\n       <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">\n        Major League Soccer\n       </a>\n       games were postponed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1626" data-file-width="1626" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Aug_27_2011_1910Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Irene shortly after landfall in the Outer Banks of North Carolina\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Southeast">\n        Southeast\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Southeast">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </a>\n       , Emergency Management was already on standby in\n       <a href="/wiki/Charleston_County,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston County, South Carolina">\n        Charleston\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Dorchester_County,_South_Carolina" title="Dorchester County, South Carolina">\n        Dorchester\n       </a>\n       counties in preparation for September. On August 23, preparations were also being made in\n       <a href="/wiki/Beaufort_County,_South_Carolina" title="Beaufort County, South Carolina">\n        Beaufort County\n       </a>\n       as well.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnaug22_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnaug22-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The gondolas were removed from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_SkyWheel" title="Myrtle Beach SkyWheel">\n        Myrtle Beach SkyWheel\n       </a>\n       attraction in preparation for tropical-storm-force winds.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       , a mandatory evacuation order was issued on August 23, for\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocracoke,_North_Carolina" title="Ocracoke, North Carolina">\n        Ocracoke Island\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hyde_County,_North_Carolina" title="Hyde County, North Carolina">\n        Hyde County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnaug22_56-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnaug22-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">\n        <a href="#cite_note-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Bev_Perdue" title="Bev Perdue">\n        Bev Perdue\n       </a>\n       declared a\n       <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">\n        state of emergency\n       </a>\n       on August 25, with hurricane and tropical storm watches posted for the state; a mandatory evacuation was issued for\n       <a href="/wiki/Carteret_County,_North_Carolina" title="Carteret County, North Carolina">\n        Carteret County\n       </a>\n       and for all tourists of\n       <a href="/wiki/Dare_County,_North_Carolina" title="Dare County, North Carolina">\n        Dare County\n       </a>\n       , though the latter was extended to include all residents by the next day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-carteretnc_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-carteretnc-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dare-county-bulletins_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-dare-county-bulletins-59">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, officials urged residents at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Bogue_Banks" title="Bogue Banks">\n        Bogue Banks\n       </a>\n       to commence evacuations by 6\xc2\xa0am August 26, and tourists in\n       <a href="/wiki/Currituck_County,_North_Carolina" title="Currituck County, North Carolina">\n        Currituck County\n       </a>\n       were advised to move inland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-carteretnc_58-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-carteretnc-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbcaug25_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbcaug25-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Seymour_Johnson_Air_Force_Base&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Seymour Johnson Air Force Base (page does not exist)">\n        Seymour Johnson Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       planned to move jets to\n       <a href="/wiki/Barksdale_Air_Force_Base" title="Barksdale Air Force Base">\n        Barksdale Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">\n        Louisiana\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">\n        <a href="#cite_note-61">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Marine_Corps_Air_Station_Cherry_Point" title="Marine Corps Air Station Cherry Point">\n        Marine Corps Air Station Cherry Point\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Marine_Corps_Air_Station_New_River" title="Marine Corps Air Station New River">\n        Marine Corps Air Station New River\n       </a>\n       both evacuated their aircraft as well.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Progress_Energy_Inc" title="Progress Energy Inc">\n        Progress Energy\n       </a>\n       announced on August 26, it would have 800 more line workers and 250 tree cutters ready after Hurricane Irene.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ap-forbes-ncoutages_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ap-forbes-ncoutages-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Officials at\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_North_Carolina_at_Wilmington" title="University of North Carolina at Wilmington">\n        UNC-Wilmington\n       </a>\n       issued a voluntary evacuation and enforced a curfew in response to the storm, interrupting move-in activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">\n        <a href="#cite_note-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As low-level atmospheric\n       <a href="/wiki/Deformation_(meteorology)#Stretching_direction" title="Deformation (meteorology)">\n        confluence\n       </a>\n       within the outer bands developed near the coast, a tornado watch was issued from north-northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Hatteras" title="Cape Hatteras">\n        Cape Hatteras\n       </a>\n       to southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">\n        Wilmington\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Virginia Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Bob_McDonnell" title="Bob McDonnell">\n        Bob McDonnell\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency in preparation for any possible effects from the hurricane along coastlines. Authorities in the cities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Norfolk,_Virginia" title="Norfolk, Virginia">\n        Norfolk\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach,_Virginia" title="Virginia Beach, Virginia">\n        Virginia Beach\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Newport_News,_Virginia" title="Newport News, Virginia">\n        Newport News\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hampton,_Virginia" title="Hampton, Virginia">\n        Hampton\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_Virginia" title="Portsmouth, Virginia">\n        Portsmouth\n       </a>\n       issued voluntary and mandatory evacuations for low-lying and oceanfront areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city of\n       <a href="/wiki/Poquoson,_Virginia" title="Poquoson, Virginia">\n        Poquoson\n       </a>\n       ordered a mandatory evacuation for all of its citizens.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">\n        <a href="#cite_note-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Public storm shelters were opened in most the cities, and officials also prepared school buildings to accommodate evacuees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnstatebystate_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnstatebystate-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By August 25, dozens of vessels at the Norfolk and Newport News shipyards began to evacuate or prepare to weather the storm, including the carriers\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(CVN-65)" title="USS Enterprise (CVN-65)">\n         Enterprise\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USS_Dwight_D._Eisenhower_(CVN-69)" title="USS Dwight D. Eisenhower (CVN-69)">\n         Dwight D. Eisenhower\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USS_Harry_S._Truman_(CVN-75)" title="USS Harry S. Truman (CVN-75)">\n         Harry S. Truman\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_(CVN-71)" title="USS Theodore Roosevelt (CVN-71)">\n         Theodore Roosevelt\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the construction site of the\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USS_Gerald_R._Ford_(CVN-78)" title="USS Gerald R. Ford (CVN-78)">\n         Gerald R. Ford\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">\n        United States Navy\n       </a>\n       ordered ships to halt their operations and clear the warning zone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbcaug25_60-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbcaug25-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Monroe" title="Fort Monroe">\n        Fort Monroe\n       </a>\n       Army base was evacuated on August 26;\n       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Base_Langley%E2%80%93Eustis" title="Joint Base Langley\xe2\x80\x93Eustis">\n        Langley Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       followed suit the next day, save essential personnel.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-transithalt_54-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-transithalt-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mid-Atlantic">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Mid-Atlantic">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1058" data-file-width="1500" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg/220px-Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg/330px-Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg/440px-Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_irene_082811_0832_edt.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Satellite image of Irene making landfall in New York City.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On August 25, Maryland Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Martin_O%27Malley" title="Martin O\'Malley">\n        Martin O\'Malley\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency in preparation for Irene.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">\n        <a href="#cite_note-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_Maryland" title="Ocean City, Maryland">\n        Ocean City\n       </a>\n       initiated "phase one" of its\n       <a href="/wiki/Contingency_plan" title="Contingency plan">\n        contingency plan\n       </a>\n       that same day, which includes a mandatory evacuation order for international workforce students.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hours later, phase three of the plan was instituted; it ordered a mandatory evacuation scheduled to start at midnight August 25, for all residents, with the requirement that everyone be evacuated by 5\xc2\xa0pm local time, August 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n        <a href="#cite_note-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 26,\n       <a href="/wiki/Dorchester_County,_Maryland" title="Dorchester County, Maryland">\n        Dorchester\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wicomico_County,_Maryland" title="Wicomico County, Maryland">\n        Wicomico\n       </a>\n       Counties declared states of emergency.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Certain geographic areas of\n       <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County,_Maryland" title="Somerset County, Maryland">\n        Somerset\n       </a>\n       and Wicomico Counties, along with all mobile homes in Wicomico County, had mandatory evacuation orders put in effect.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Public shelters were made available in Dorchester,\n       <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County,_Maryland" title="Somerset County, Maryland">\n        Somerset\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Wicomico_County,_Maryland" title="Wicomico County, Maryland">\n        Wicomico\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Worcester_County,_Maryland" title="Worcester County, Maryland">\n        Worcester\n       </a>\n       Counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       , Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Jack_Markell" title="Jack Markell">\n        Jack Markell\n       </a>\n       ordered visitors to evacuate the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delaware_beaches" title="Delaware beaches">\n        Delaware beaches\n       </a>\n       effective 6:00\xc2\xa0pm on August 25. In addition, he declared a state of emergency; shelters were scheduled to open throughout the state on August 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-do_41-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-do-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_May_%E2%80%93_Lewes_Ferry" title="Cape May \xe2\x80\x93 Lewes Ferry">\n        Cape May\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 Lewes Ferry\n       </a>\n       across\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Bay" title="Delaware Bay">\n        Delaware Bay\n       </a>\n       also suspended service for late August 27, through August 28, in response to the pending arrival of the hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kyw_80-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-kyw-80">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Toll operations on\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Route_1" title="Delaware Route 1">\n        Delaware Route 1\n       </a>\n       were halted in order to optimize evacuation rates along highways. Transit services were expected to be shut down on August 27 and 28, while bridges over the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chesapeake_and_Delaware_Canal" title="Chesapeake and Delaware Canal">\n        Chesapeake and Delaware Canal\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Indian_River_(Delaware)" title="Indian River (Delaware)">\n        Indian River\n       </a>\n       were closed due to high wind.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-do2_82-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-do2-82">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A tornado watch was issued for Delaware in association with Irene at 10:40\xc2\xa0am August 27.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twatchdel_83-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twatchdel-83">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg/220px-Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg/330px-Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg/440px-Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irene_Boarded_Windows.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A restaurant boards up in preparation for Irene in\n         <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_New_Jersey" title="Ocean City, New Jersey">\n          Ocean City, New Jersey\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n       , the forecast arrival of Hurricane Irene caused postponement of the planned August 28 dedication ceremony for the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Martin_Luther_King,_Jr._National_Memorial" title="Martin Luther King, Jr. National Memorial">\n        Martin Luther King, Jr. National Memorial\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In anticipation of the storm, thousands of sandbags were prepared for placement at flood-prone\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington_Metro" title="Washington Metro">\n        Washington Metro\n       </a>\n       station entrances.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washpost26_40-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washpost26-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">\n        Amtrak\n       </a>\n       service from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Station_(Washington,_D.C.)" title="Union Station (Washington, D.C.)">\n        Washington\'s Union Station\n       </a>\n       southward was cancelled from August 26, until August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       , the ground was already saturated with water when the hurricane arrived, since the preceding month had been the wettest ever recorded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MyFoxPhilly01_85-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MyFoxPhilly01-85">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Philadelphia mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Nutter" title="Michael Nutter">\n        Michael Nutter\n       </a>\n       expressed concern that there could be severe devastation in the city and surrounding areas,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Tom_Corbett" title="Tom Corbett">\n        Tom Corbett\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency in Pennsylvania.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/SEPTA" title="SEPTA">\n        Southeastern Pennsylvania Transportation Authority\n       </a>\n       decided to halt all commuter rail service after midnight August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-transithalt_54-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-transithalt-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 26, Philadelphia\'s mayor announced there would be no mandatory evacuations for the city, but urged residents to be prudent and to take action and leave should conditions warrant.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Officials prepared to open three large shelters on the evening of August 27, capable of holding up to 6,000 people. The Philadelphia International Airport closed at 10:30\xc2\xa0pm on Saturday and remained closed until Monday.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-do2_82-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-do2-82">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Hook,_Pennsylvania" title="Marcus Hook, Pennsylvania">\n        Marcus Hook\n       </a>\n       , along the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">\n        Delaware River\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sunoco" title="Sunoco">\n        Sunoco\n       </a>\n       oil refinery preemptively lowered its production rate by 25\xc2\xa0percent, to 140,000 barrels per day (22,000\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        3\n       </sup>\n       /d).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sunocoreduced_89-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sunocoreduced-89">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg/220px-GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg/330px-GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg/440px-GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:GrandCentralTerminalEmpty.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Grand_Central_Terminal" title="Grand Central Terminal">\n          Grand Central Terminal\n         </a>\n         stands empty following shut down of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Metro-North_Railroad" title="Metro-North Railroad">\n          Metro-North Railroad\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       , Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Chris_Christie" title="Chris Christie">\n        Chris Christie\n       </a>\n       declared a\n       <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">\n        state of emergency\n       </a>\n       on August 25,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tsl_90-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tsl-90">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with President Obama reaffirming the declaration nationally by August 27.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mandatory evacuations were ordered for all of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_May_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cape May County, New Jersey">\n        Cape May County\n       </a>\n       and all\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_County,_New_Jersey" title="Atlantic County, New Jersey">\n        Atlantic County\n       </a>\n       shore communities east of\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_9_in_New_Jersey" title="U.S. Route 9 in New Jersey">\n        Route 9\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       prompting\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_City,_New_Jersey" title="Atlantic City, New Jersey">\n        Atlantic City\n       </a>\n       \'s first evacuation in history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About 1,500\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Army_National_Guard" title="New Jersey Army National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       troops were deployed in New Jersey. One National Guard outfit was deployed to flood-prone Manville, NJ, (which was also devastated by Hurricane Floyd in 1999) A couple of National Guardsman attempted to drive two of their deep-water-capable\n       <a href="/wiki/Family_of_Medium_Tactical_Vehicles" title="Family of Medium Tactical Vehicles">\n        FMTVs\n       </a>\n       through the flooding, but the floodwaters were too deep. The vehicles were overtaken by the waters beneath a dipping Conrail underpass on South Main Street. The Guardsmen were photographed and videotaped by onlookers above them on the train bridge, and both photos and videos went viral over social media.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_94-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mandatory evacuations were also ordered for all of\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Beach_Island" title="Long Beach Island">\n        Long Beach Island\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_County,_New_Jersey" title="Ocean County, New Jersey">\n        Ocean County\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Barnegat_Peninsula" title="Barnegat Peninsula">\n        Barnegat Peninsula\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       To relieve evacuation traffic, toll operations were temporarily suspended on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Garden_State_Parkway" title="Garden State Parkway">\n        Garden State Parkway\n       </a>\n       south of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Raritan_River" title="Raritan River">\n        Raritan River\n       </a>\n       and on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_City_Expressway" title="Atlantic City Expressway">\n        Atlantic City Expressway\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnstatebystate_68-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnstatebystate-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Residents of low-lying areas of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_County,_New_Jersey" title="Hudson County, New Jersey">\n        Hudson County\n       </a>\n       along the\n       <a href="/wiki/North_River_(Hudson_River)" title="North River (Hudson River)">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Upper_New_York_Bay" title="Upper New York Bay">\n        Upper New York Bay\n       </a>\n       were advised to evacuate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_New_York" title="Governor of New York">\n        Governor of New York\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Cuomo" title="Andrew Cuomo">\n        Andrew Cuomo\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on August 26,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and that day issued a mandatory evacuation order for low-lying areas of New York City.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnliveblog_48-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnliveblog-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-evac-order-nyc_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-evac-order-nyc-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A day prior, New York City Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Bloomberg" title="Michael Bloomberg">\n        Michael Bloomberg\n       </a>\n       had announced that the city would prepare to create "an enormous shelter system" for residents without access to higher ground.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bloombergstatement_100-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bloombergstatement-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President Barack Obama issued a state of emergency declaration for the New York metropolitan area, freeing federal disaster funds, and tasking the\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n        Federal Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Department_of_Homeland_Security" title="Department of Homeland Security">\n        Department of Homeland Security\n       </a>\n       to coordinate disaster relief efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Cuomo deployed 2,000 National Guard troops to assist police, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Transportation_Authority" title="Metropolitan Transportation Authority">\n        Metropolitan Transportation Authority\n       </a>\n       (MTA) and the Port Authority in New York and\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Island" title="Long Island">\n        Long Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_94-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Possible rising seawater levels from storm surge and a predicted high tide led to a complete shutdown of the MTA, the nation\'s largest mass transit system. All\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_Subway" title="New York City Subway">\n        subway\n       </a>\n       , bus, and commuter rail service in New York City was halted\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       at noon on August 27.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-transithalt_54-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-transithalt-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Four area hospitals began evacuating patients on August 26;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnliveblog_48-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnliveblog-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-transithalt_54-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-transithalt-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnstatebystate_68-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnstatebystate-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       sixteen nursing homes and adult care facilities were also evacuated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnnstatebystate_68-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cnnstatebystate-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_International_Fringe_Festival" title="New York International Fringe Festival">\n        New York International Fringe Festival\n       </a>\n       cancelled all performances for August 27, and 28, as did all Broadway shows for those days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Tennis_Association" title="United States Tennis Association">\n        United States Tennis Association\n       </a>\n       cancelled special events planned for the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_US_Open_(tennis)" title="2011 US Open (tennis)">\n        2011 US Open\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_England">\n        New England\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: New England">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="1944" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg/220px-HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg/330px-HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg/440px-HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:HurricaneIrene_2011_BefdordBasinVessels.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Vessels riding out the storm in Bedford Basin near Halifax, Nova Scotia\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Southern\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       , along the\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Island_Sound" title="Long Island Sound">\n        Long Island Sound\n       </a>\n       , had a hurricane warning in place as of August 27, while northern Connecticut had a tropical storm warning.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Connecticut" title="Governor of Connecticut">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Dannel_Malloy" title="Dannel Malloy">\n        Dannel Malloy\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjblog_44-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjblog-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the state\'s emergency operations center was fully activated. As of 11\xc2\xa0a.m. on August 26, about 33,000 sandbags had been distributed to state residents. Bridgeport sustained heavier damages and many parts of south Groton had numerous power outages which took weeks to get up back and running.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2011)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island" title="Rhode Island">\n        Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       , the Army Corps of Engineers closed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Fox_Point_Hurricane_Barrier" title="Fox Point Hurricane Barrier">\n        Fox Point Hurricane Barrier\n       </a>\n       in anticipation that the hurricane would make a direct strike on\n       <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">\n        Providence\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Massachusetts" title="Governor of Massachusetts">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Deval_Patrick" title="Deval Patrick">\n        Deval Patrick\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on August 26, activated 500\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_National_Guard" title="Massachusetts National Guard">\n        Massachusetts National Guard\n       </a>\n       troops, and also planned to activate an additional 2,000 troops the following day in preparation for the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In an unprecedented move, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Massachusetts_Bay_Transit_Authority" title="Massachusetts Bay Transit Authority">\n        MBTA\n       </a>\n       suspended all metropolitan Boston public transportation at 8:00\xc2\xa0am on August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Vermont" title="Governor of Vermont">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Peter_Shumlin" title="Peter Shumlin">\n        Peter Shumlin\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on August 27, in preparation for the hurricane\'s arrival.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wcax_47-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wcax-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In a joint statement, Vermont electric utilities announced that they planned to have extra staff on hand.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">\n        National Weather Service\n       </a>\n       stated that it anticipated 2\xe2\x80\x935 inches (51\xe2\x80\x93127\xc2\xa0mm) of rain on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Champlain_Valley" title="Champlain Valley">\n        Champlain Valley\n       </a>\n       and western Vermont and 3\xe2\x80\x937 inches (76\xe2\x80\x93178\xc2\xa0mm) in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Green_Mountains" title="Green Mountains">\n        Green Mountains\n       </a>\n       and eastern Vermont, with the risk of flooding near streams and rivers and an anticipated sustained\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_speed" title="Wind speed">\n        wind speeds\n       </a>\n       of 30\xe2\x80\x9345 miles per hour (48\xe2\x80\x9372\xc2\xa0km/h) and gusts of up to 45\xe2\x80\x9365 miles per hour (72\xe2\x80\x93105\xc2\xa0km/h), causing significant tree damage and damage to\n       <a href="/wiki/Overhead_power_line" title="Overhead power line">\n        power lines\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Maine" title="Governor of Maine">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Paul_LePage" title="Paul LePage">\n        Paul LePage\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on August 26, in preparation for the expected arrival of Hurricane Irene on August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mueller_49-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mueller-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Canadian utility and line workers were dispatched to Maine to assist in reinforcing the state\'s electrical infrastructure.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mueller_49-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mueller-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ten shelters were to be opened in Maine.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">\n        Canada\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Canada">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Near\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Halifax_Regional_Municipality" title="Halifax Regional Municipality">\n        Halifax\n       </a>\n       , Nova Scotia, Canada, numerous large local and ocean-going vessels anchored in\n       <a href="/wiki/Bedford_Basin" title="Bedford Basin">\n        Bedford Basin\n       </a>\n       to ride out the storm.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2011)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Impact">\n        Impact\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n          Puerto Rico\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7000100000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">\n          0 !\n         </span>\n         <span class="sorttext">\n          None\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7008500000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $500\xc2\xa0million\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-6">\n          <a
