     </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="sortbottom">\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          Totals:\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          49\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          9\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010165000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $16.5\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lesser_Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Lesser Antilles">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Following its path through the northeastern Caribbean, Irene spread tropical storm conditions across all of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">\n        Leeward Islands\n       </a>\n       , causing overall little damage but flooded some low-lying areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       To the south, strong thunderstorms and showers spread over\n       <a href="/wiki/Martinique" title="Martinique">\n        Martinique\n       </a>\n       , though most of the activity occurred prior to development into a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In spite of the center tracking just north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">\n        Guadeloupe\n       </a>\n       \'s island\n       <a href="/wiki/Grande-Terre" title="Grande-Terre">\n        Grande-Terre\n       </a>\n       , the strongest effects were brought on by Irene\'s outer\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">\n        rainbands\n       </a>\n       . Tropical-storm-force winds generated brief rough seas, with peak\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_wave" title="Wind wave">\n        wave\n       </a>\n       heights of no more than 18\xc2\xa0ft (5.5\xc2\xa0m). Accompanying intermittent torrents swept through much of the territory, but overall rainfall was moderate; precipitation totals of between 3.1 and 4.7\xc2\xa0in (79 and 119\xc2\xa0mm) fell in\n       <a href="/wiki/Basse-Terre_Island" title="Basse-Terre Island">\n        Basse-Terre\n       </a>\n       during the event.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to the storm conditions,\n       <a href="/wiki/LIAT" title="LIAT">\n        LIAT\n       </a>\n       was forced to suspend all of its flights in\n       <a href="/wiki/Antigua" title="Antigua">\n        Antigua\n       </a>\n       for early August 22.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Passing near the\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Virgin_Islands" title="British Virgin Islands">\n        British Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       while strengthening, Irene brought gusty winds and heavy precipitation to the territory; however, resultant property damage was minimal.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n        <a href="#cite_note-117">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A lightning strike over\n       <a href="/wiki/Necker_Island_(British_Virgin_Islands)" title="Necker Island (British Virgin Islands)">\n        Necker Island\n       </a>\n       sparked a large fire at one of business magnate\n       <a href="/wiki/Richard_Branson" title="Richard Branson">\n        Richard Branson\n       </a>\n       \'s resort homes, but all of its guest occupants\xe2\x80\x94including British actress\n       <a href="/wiki/Kate_Winslet" title="Kate Winslet">\n        Kate Winslet\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94were able to exit the area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Irene crossed\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Croix,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Croix, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint Croix, U.S. Virgin Islands\n       </a>\n       as a strong tropical storm on August 21, though relatively calm winds associated with the passage of its center were recorded over the island. To the north in\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Thomas,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Thomas, U.S. Virgin Islands">\n        Saint Thomas\n       </a>\n       , storm conditions became progressively worse; sustained gale-force winds swept across the territory, with a gust of up to 68\xc2\xa0mph (109\xc2\xa0km/h) recorded at 21:20 UTC. Upon impact, the winds and inclement weather caused scattered power outages across all islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vidn_32-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-vidn-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Wide-scale assessments confirmed light damage to public schools, mostly confined to debris and leaks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Greater_Antilles">\n        Greater Antilles\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Greater Antilles">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Puerto_Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Puerto Rico">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1132" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif/220px-Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif/330px-Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif/440px-Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_Puerto_Rico_rainfall.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Irene\'s rainfall across Puerto Rico\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Across Puerto Rico, heavy rains caused extensive damage to roads while hurricane-force winds toppled many trees and utility poles, leaving more than 1\xc2\xa0million residences without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-elregional_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-elregional-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Forbes_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Forbes-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        Barack Obama\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nydn1_122-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nydn1-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About 121,000 customers were cut off from potable water service at the height of the storm, and islandwide at least 771 people had to take shelter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-elregional_120-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-elregional-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">\n        <a href="#cite_note-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At higher elevations, winds estimated by\n       <a href="/wiki/Weather_radar" title="Weather radar">\n        radar\n       </a>\n       neared 111\xc2\xa0mph (179\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The highest amounts of precipitation fell across eastern parts of the territory; in\n       <a href="/wiki/Gurabo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Gurabo, Puerto Rico">\n        Gurabo\n       </a>\n       , a peak total of 22.04\xc2\xa0in (560\xc2\xa0mm) was recorded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">\n        <a href="#cite_note-125">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several rivers burst their banks as a consequence of the rains, causing additional flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Forbes_121-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Forbes-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The agricultural sector also suffered losses from the storm, particularly near the location of landfall. High winds uprooted crop plants, and several coffee and banana plantations sustained minor damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Of the plantations, the most affected were situated in\n       <a href="/wiki/Yabucoa,_Puerto_Rico" title="Yabucoa, Puerto Rico">\n        Yabucoa\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Maunabo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Maunabo, Puerto Rico">\n        Maunabo\n       </a>\n       , where severe flooding washed out copious amounts of banana crop.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The rains continued to fall for hours into the wake of the storm, prompting the issuance of flood watches.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In total, Irene affected over 1,500 people in Puerto Rico, and one driver was killed after their vehicle was caught in swollen currents.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Preliminary estimates indicate structural damage could be as high as $500 million (USD), with additional losses due to the three-day labor suspensions pinned at over $60.4 million (USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="7200" data-file-width="5600" height="283" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Aug_22_2011.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Image of Irene showing storm clouds covering part of the Dominican Republic and all of Puerto Rico.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Offshore near\n       <a href="/wiki/Culebra,_Puerto_Rico" title="Culebra, Puerto Rico">\n        Culebra Island\n       </a>\n       , a sailboat was reported sunken due to rough seas prior to landfall in mainland Puerto Rico. Gale-force winds felled fences and shattered windows, with a flying object piercing through one residence. A total of 46\xc2\xa0locals sought refuge to ride out the storm, but one family required post-storm shelter after the roof to their home was lost.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n        <a href="#cite_note-131">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On the island of\n       <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">\n        Vieques\n       </a>\n       , similar sustained winds of 51\xc2\xa0mph (82\xc2\xa0km/h) were recorded, as well as some gusts of up to 71\xc2\xa0mph (114\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n        <a href="#cite_note-132">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Some power and telephone service cutoffs were reported, and the island\'s airport halted its operations.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">\n        <a href="#cite_note-133">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Hispaniola">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Skirting barely north past\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </a>\n       , the large storm produced gales and prolonged precipitation in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       , displacing over 37,700 people and leaving at least 88 communities isolated in its wake.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">\n        <a href="#cite_note-134">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-damage_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-damage-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Accompanying\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        storm surge\n       </a>\n       affected roughly 200 homes and prompted evacuations along the northern coastlines.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The strongest winds also occurred in northern\n       <a href="/wiki/Cibao" title="Cibao">\n        Cibao\n       </a>\n       , where they felled multiple trees and toppled utility poles. Swollen rivers, creeks, and streams caused widespread residential flooding and damage to roads; saturated soil in the region triggered mudslides, causing additional disruptions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite its distance, Irene produced extreme rainfall in southern parts of the country that led to many secondary effects. Resultant floods combined with two overflown rivers swept through much of\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Crist%C3%B3bal,_Dominican_Republic" title="San Crist\xc3\xb3bal, Dominican Republic">\n        San Crist\xc3\xb3bal\n       </a>\n       , causing one bridge to collapse under the rushing waters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The flooding produced at least two drown victims in that area, both later confirmed dead. Elsewhere, another fatality occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cambita_Garabitos" title="Cambita Garabitos">\n        Cambita Garabitos\n       </a>\n       , and six others were listed as missing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Heavy rains also fell across\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Altagracia_Province" title="La Altagracia Province">\n        La Altagracia Province\n       </a>\n       , where one person in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hig%C3%BCey_(city)" title="Hig\xc3\xbcey (city)">\n        Hig\xc3\xbcey\n       </a>\n       went missing and hundreds were evacuated. Most of the damage in the region occurred due to flooded rivers, with some agricultural losses reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The excess surface waters overwhelmed and damaged some 170 inlets.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">\n        <a href="#cite_note-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In all, Irene affected at least 2,292 households according to preliminary reports, with 16 houses rendered beyond repair.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-damage_135-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-damage-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The associated monetary losses surmounted\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_peso" title="Dominican peso">\n        RD$\n       </a>\n       1 billion (US$30 million) in the wake of the event.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">\n        <a href="#cite_note-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In northeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       , the prolonged precipitation overflowed rivers and produced surface floods and damaging landslides across multiple road sections.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">\n        <a href="#cite_note-143">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About 500 residents in risk zones evacuated while some sought shelter, but only one of more than 160 evacuation sites required usage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UNNews_144-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-UNNews-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rough surge produced high coastal flooding, with some reports of thousands of damaged homes. In the vicinity of\n       <a href="/wiki/Port-au-Prince" title="Port-au-Prince">\n        Port-au-Prince\n       </a>\n       , brisk winds blew down many refuge tents home to victims from the major\n       <a href="/wiki/2010_Haiti_earthquake" title="2010 Haiti earthquake">\n        January 12, 2010 earthquake\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">\n        <a href="#cite_note-145">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall, officials indicated impact was less severe than initially feared; the storm only left isolated flood damage in its wake, particularly throughout northern parts of the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UNNews_144-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-UNNews-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, two people lost their lives after being caught in swollen rivers, and four others suffered injuries.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Cuba">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       As Irene was tracking through the Bahamas, the outerbands of the storm dropped light rainfall in eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       . The cities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Moa,_Cuba" title="Moa, Cuba">\n        Moa\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sagua_de_T%C3%A1namo,_Cuba" title="Sagua de T\xc3\xa1namo, Cuba">\n        Sagua de T\xc3\xa1namo\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Holgu%C3%ADn_Province" title="Holgu\xc3\xadn Province">\n        Holgu\xc3\xadn Province\n       </a>\n       reported 2.36\xc2\xa0in (60\xc2\xa0mm) of rain. However, the average rainfall throughout the Holgu\xc3\xadn Province did not exceed 0.20\xc2\xa0in (5.1\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Some damage occurred throughout\n       <a href="/wiki/Guant%C3%A1namo_Province" title="Guant\xc3\xa1namo Province">\n        Guant\xc3\xa1namo Province\n       </a>\n       , where rough surf and rains caused flooding in\n       <a href="/wiki/Baracoa" title="Baracoa">\n        Baracoa\n       </a>\n       . In addition, waves of 10 to 12 feet (3.0 to 3.7\xc2\xa0m) high were seen in Gibara, Holgu\xc3\xadn, on Wednesday 24, when Irene\'s eye was located between Acklins and Crooked Islands, Bahamas, just 178 miles (286\xc2\xa0km) northeast of the city. The strong waves, combined with high tide, caused a slight coastal flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Turks_and_Caicos_and_the_Bahamas">\n        Turks and Caicos and the Bahamas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Turks and Caicos and the Bahamas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Turks and Caicos:\n       </b>\n       On August 24, Irene passed over the\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">\n        British Overseas Territory\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">\n        Turks and Caicos Islands\n       </a>\n       at Category 1 strength. The hurricane produced high winds that blew off roofs and downed power lines throughout the territory.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Cockburn_Town" title="Cockburn Town">\n        Cockburn Town\n       </a>\n       , residences reported loss of power, and light poles were toppled. Many homes on\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Turk_Island" title="Grand Turk Island">\n        Grand Turk Island\n       </a>\n       also reported a loss of electricity during Irene\'s passage, although structural damage in the area was limited.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-foxnews_150-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-foxnews-150">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The strongest of the rains and gusts occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Providenciales" title="Providenciales">\n        Providenciales\n       </a>\n       , where light wind damage was reported to roofs and resorts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">\n        <a href="#cite_note-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Grand Turk cruise port also sustained some minor damage from the storm, but operations resumed three days after impact.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Bahamas:\n       </b>\n       A major hurricane, Irene trekked right through\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Bahamas" title="The Bahamas">\n        the Bahamas\n       </a>\n       , with its eye making landfall on several of the islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wsjaug25_39-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wsjaug25-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A peak wind gust of about 140\xc2\xa0mph (230\xc2\xa0km/h) was recorded at the height of the storm, and localized heavy rains of up to 13 inches (330\xc2\xa0mm) fell in the area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-worst_153-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-worst-153">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The extreme winds damaged at least 40 homes on\n       <a href="/wiki/Mayaguana" title="Mayaguana">\n        Mayaguana Island\n       </a>\n       , and dozens of homes on\n       <a href="/wiki/Acklins" title="Acklins">\n        Acklins\n       </a>\n       were completely obliterated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbcaug25_60-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbcaug25-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On the latter island, the hurricane reportedly wiped out 90 percent of the\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Lovely_Bay,_Acklins&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Lovely Bay, Acklins (page does not exist)">\n        Lovely Bay\n       </a>\n       settlement.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Similar winds tore off the roof and shattered the windows out of a high school on\n       <a href="/wiki/Crooked_Island,_Bahamas" title="Crooked Island, Bahamas">\n        Crooked Island\n       </a>\n       , where wind gusts as high as 99\xc2\xa0mph (159\xc2\xa0km/h) were reported.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">\n        <a href="#cite_note-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As well, a local church on the island partially collapsed due to the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNN_156-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNN-156">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The worst of the destruction occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cat_Island,_Bahamas" title="Cat Island, Bahamas">\n        Cat Island\n       </a>\n       , characterized by widespread shattered glass and torn houses. In all, the storm caused "millions of dollars" worth in structural damage on the island, and left many homeless.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">\n        <a href="#cite_note-157">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Across\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Providence" title="New Providence">\n        New Providence\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Bahama" title="Grand Bahama">\n        Grand Bahama\n       </a>\n       , only limited impact occurred as Irene remained well offshore; businesses operations were scheduled to return to normal shortly after the storm. Nationwide, the damage was estimated at $40\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BahamasDamage_111-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-BahamasDamage-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite the overall extensive structural damage inflicted, there were no reports of fatalities on the islands in the wake of disaster.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNN_156-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNN-156">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_2">\n        United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:247px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_rainfall.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="993" data-file-width="649" height="375" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Irene_2011_rainfall.gif/245px-Irene_2011_rainfall.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Irene_2011_rainfall.gif/368px-Irene_2011_rainfall.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Irene_2011_rainfall.gif/490px-Irene_2011_rainfall.gif 2x" width="245"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irene_2011_rainfall.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Storm total rainfall from Hurricane Irene\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <table align="left" border="1" class="wikitable" style=\'"margin:0\'>\n       <caption>\n        <a href="/wiki/List_of_costliest_Atlantic_hurricanes"       </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2017\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7011198000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $198\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n hurricane season">\n          2012\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010714000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $71.4\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         4\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">\n          Ike\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2008\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010295200000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $29.5\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         5\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Andrew" title="Hurricane Andrew">\n          Andrew\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/1992_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1992 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          1992\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010265000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $26.5\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         6\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Wilma" title="Hurricane Wilma">\n          Wilma\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010210070000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $21\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         7\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ivan" title="Hurricane Ivan">\n          Ivan\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2004_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2004 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2004\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010188200000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $18.8\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         8\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">\n          Irene\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2011\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010156000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $15.6\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         9\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Charley" title="Hurricane Charley">\n          Charley\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2004_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2004 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2004\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010151130000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $15.1\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         10\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rita" title="Hurricane Rita">\n          Rita\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7010120370000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $12\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="small">\n        <th colspan="6">\n         Source: National Hurricane Center\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dead_2011_158-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-Dead_2011-158">\n           [158]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">\n          <a href="#cite_note-159">\n           [159]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">\n          <a href="#cite_note-160">\n           [160]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">\n          <a href="#cite_note-161">\n           [nb 1]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Gales from Irene affected nearly all of the Eastern Seaboard, extending from Florida to New England and as far inland as central New York and central Pennsylvania, affecting all or large parts of 15 states and the District of Columbia. The winds, combined with soil saturation due to the extreme amounts of precipitation in many of the impacted areas both from Irene and from previous thunderstorms, uprooted countless trees and power lines along the storm\'s path. Roughly 7.4 million homes and businesses lost electrical power, with approximately 3.3 million still without power as of August 30, three days after landfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">\n        <a href="#cite_note-162">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Coastal areas suffered extensive flood damage followings its potent storm surge, with additional freshwater flooding reported in many areas. The storm spawned scattered tornadoes, causing significant property damage as evidenced by destroyed homes. In the\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeastern_United_States" title="Northeastern United States">\n        northeastern region\n       </a>\n       , more than ten rivers measured record flood heights at their\n       <a href="/wiki/Hydrograph" title="Hydrograph">\n        hydrographs\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rivers in at least six Northeastern states reached\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hundred-year_flood" title="Hundred-year flood">\n        hundred-year flood\n       </a>\n       levels, while the flooding in\n       <a href="/wiki/Greene_County,_New_York" title="Greene County, New York">\n        Greene County, New York\n       </a>\n       was described as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/500-year_flood" title="500-year flood">\n        five-hundred-year-flood conditions\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">\n        <a href="#cite_note-164">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding in\n       <a href="/wiki/Schoharie_County,_New_York" title="Schoharie County, New York">\n        Schoharie County, New York\n       </a>\n       was also reported by the National Weather Service in Albany, New York as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/500-year_flood" title="500-year flood">\n        five-hundred-year-flood conditions\n       </a>\n       . Throughout its path in the contiguous United States, Irene caused approximately $15.6 billion (2011 USD) in damage and 47 deaths.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">\n        <a href="#cite_note-166">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Southeast_2">\n        Southeast\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Southeast">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Florida">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Though Irene spared Florida from a direct hit, its outernmost rainbands produced squalls and intermittent torrents along the state\'s eastern coastlines. Brisk winds produced scattered power outages\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPTV_167-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPTV-167">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">\n          <span title="The material near this tag failed verification of its source citation(s). (October 2011)">\n           not in citation given\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       and waves reaching as high as 12\xc2\xa0ft (3.7\xc2\xa0m);\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPTV_167-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPTV-167">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       rough surf in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Boynton_Inlet" title="Boynton Inlet">\n        Boynton Inlet\n       </a>\n       injured at least eight people,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">\n        <a href="#cite_note-168">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and two surfers were killed offshore\n       <a href="/wiki/Volusia_County,_Florida" title="Volusia County, Florida">\n        Volusia County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">\n        <a href="#cite_note-169">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Elsewhere, in\n       <a href="/wiki/Lantana,_Florida" title="Lantana, Florida">\n        Lantana\n       </a>\n       , large waves sweeping over seawalls went on to destroy a lifeguard tower.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">\n        <a href="#cite_note-170">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Localized beach erosion was also reported, although it was not significant.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPTV_167-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPTV-167">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Onshore, comparatively light winds brushed the state; the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Worth,_Florida" title="Lake Worth, Florida">\n        Lake Worth\n       </a>\n       pier reporting a peak gust of 40\xc2\xa0mph (64\xc2\xa0km/h), with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_International_Airport" title="Palm Beach International Airport">\n        Palm Beach International Airport\n       </a>\n       recording winds of no more than 31\xc2\xa0mph (50\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPTV_167-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPTV-167">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Precipitation in the area was also light, with a peak accumulation of 2.67 inches (68\xc2\xa0mm) recorded at\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale_Executive_Airport" title="Fort Lauderdale Executive Airport">\n        Fort Lauderdale Executive Airport\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">\n        <a href="#cite_note-171">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Further north, rainfall from the storm totaled no more than 1.31 inches (33\xc2\xa0mm) on August 24 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Melbourne,_Florida" title="Melbourne, Florida">\n        Melbourne\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">\n        <a href="#cite_note-172">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="South_Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: South Carolina">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Owing to its unusually large windfield, Irene affected long stretches of\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </a>\n       coastlines with gusts and sporadic heavy showers, even though it remained offshore. Gale-force winds picked up through the\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina_Lowcountry" title="South Carolina Lowcountry">\n        Lowcountry\n       </a>\n       during the afternoon of August 26, with a gust of 55\xc2\xa0mph (89\xc2\xa0km/h) measured at a coastal marine observing site on\n       <a href="/wiki/Folly_Island" title="Folly Island">\n        Folly Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-powerout_173-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-powerout-173">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Scattered power outages left over 4,000 residences in the dark, mostly due to toppled utility poles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">\n        <a href="#cite_note-174">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The winds also felled trees and generated rough surf along\n       <a href="/wiki/Charleston_County,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston County, South Carolina">\n        Charleston County\n       </a>\n       coastlines, and minor beach erosion was noted. Elsewhere in that county, a downed tree trapped several people in their vehicle, but they were all rescued.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-powerout_173-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-powerout-173">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="North_Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: North Carolina">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Tropical-storm-force winds began to affect the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       hours before landfall, producing waves of 6\xe2\x80\x939\xc2\xa0ft (1.8\xe2\x80\x932.7\xc2\xa0m).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bostonglobeaug26_175-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bostonglobeaug26-175">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition to the gales, Irene spawned several\n       <a href="/wiki/Tornado" title="Tornado">\n        tornadoes\n       </a>\n       early on August 27, while approaching the coast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">\n        <a href="#cite_note-176">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       No regular weather station or\n       <a href="/wiki/Weather_buoy" title="Weather buoy">\n        buoy\n       </a>\n       , however, measured sustained hurricane-force winds from the storm, with the highest winds officially recorded at 67\xc2\xa0mph (108\xc2\xa0km/h) by a buoy near\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Lookout,_North_Carolina" title="Cape Lookout, North Carolina">\n        Cape Lookout\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Precipitation totals from Irene in the region were particularly high, ranging between 10\xe2\x80\x9314 inches (250\xe2\x80\x93360\xc2\xa0mm); Bunyan recorded a peak amount of approximately 14 inches (360\xc2\xa0mm).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis30A_29-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis30A-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The large hurricane left extensive damage in its wake and produced tornadoes that damaged homes and overturned vehicles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-treeso_179-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-treeso-179">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the touch down of a potent tornado, at least four homes were demolished in\n       <a href="/wiki/Columbia,_North_Carolina" title="Columbia, North Carolina">\n        Columbia\n       </a>\n       , while up to three others sustained significant damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">\n        <a href="#cite_note-180">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The hurricane caused multiple flooded areas and uprooted trees along coastlines;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-treeso_179-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-treeso-179">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nash_County,_North_Carolina" title="Nash County, North Carolina">\n        Nash County\n       </a>\n       , a snatched tree limb struck and killed one person.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181">\n        <a href="#cite_note-181">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Prior to the storm, a resident in\n       <a href="/wiki/Onslow_County,_North_Carolina" title="Onslow County, North Carolina">\n        Onslow County\n       </a>\n       suffered a fatal heart attack while applying plywood to his house.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182">\n        <a href="#cite_note-182">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two people in\n       <a href="/wiki/Pitt_County,_North_Carolina" title="Pitt County, North Carolina">\n        Pitt\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Sampson_County,_North_Carolina" title="Sampson County, North Carolina">\n        Sampson\n       </a>\n       Counties were additionally killed by falling trees, as were two others in\n       <a href="/wiki/Goldsboro,_North_Carolina" title="Goldsboro, North Carolina">\n        Goldsboro\n       </a>\n       and Pitt County in traffic accidents. A man also drowned in the flooded\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Fear_River" title="Cape Fear River">\n        Cape Fear River\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In all, over 1,100 homes were destroyed. The estimated $71 million in damage did not include agricultural losses.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Irene cut several breaches across\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina_Highway_12" title="North Carolina Highway 12">\n        North Carolina Highway 12\n       </a>\n       on\n       <a href="/wiki/Hatteras_Island" title="Hatteras Island">\n        Hatteras Island\n       </a>\n       , isolating the island from the rest of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       . Several of the smaller breaches were filled in with sand, but the largest, which is 200 feet (61\xc2\xa0m) wide, was left open, recreating\n       <a href="/wiki/Pea_Island" title="Pea Island">\n        Pea Island\n       </a>\n       for the first time since 1945. As a result, the only way to access Hatteras Island was by ferry. On October 10, 2011, a temporary 662-foot-long (202\xc2\xa0m) bridge opened over the breach. The bridge could be in place for more than 10 years while other solutions are considered.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hr101011_184-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-hr101011-184">\n         [183]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The path of the hurricane was thought by many to be the\n       <a href="/wiki/Scenario_planning" title="Scenario planning">\n        worst-case scenario\n       </a>\n       for the Outer Banks, just east over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pamlico_Sound" title="Pamlico Sound">\n        Pamlico Sound\n       </a>\n       . The storm winds pushed the water rushing into the sound in the form of rainfall back up the rivers feeding the sound and when the hurricane passed the water rushed back out causing historic flooding along the Outer Banks in particular in the towns of Waves, Rodanthe and Salvo. The flood caused major damage to the area that can still be seen in\n       <a class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/mirlobeachnc/hurricane-irene-damage-to-mirlo-beach" rel="nofollow">\n        Mirlo Beach\n       </a>\n       at the north end of Rodanthe. Flood waters exceeded seven feet in many locations and destroyed many houses and businesses.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 165.33333333333px">\n        <div style="width: 165.33333333333px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 163.33333333333px;">\n          <div style="margin:0px auto;">\n           <a   </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Radar image of the storm at landfall in the Outer Banks of North Carolina.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           The astronauts on board the ISS captured this series of still frames as Hurricane Irene, a category 1 storm at the time, made landfall into the coast of North Carolina.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a  </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_(6094141162).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165"
