srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_%286094141162%29.jpg/330px-Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_%286094141162%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_%286094141162%29.jpg/440px-Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_%286094141162%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Flooded_boardwalk_near_Toms_Cove_Visitor_Center_(6094141162).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Flooding at\n         <a href="/wiki/Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Chincoteague National Wildlife Refuge">\n          Chincoteague National Wildlife Refuge\n         </a>\n         on\n         <a href="/wiki/Assateague_Island" title="Assateague Island">\n          Assateague Island\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A tornado moved through the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandbridge,_Virginia_Beach,_Virginia" title="Sandbridge, Virginia Beach, Virginia">\n        Sandbridge\n       </a>\n       community in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach" title="Virginia Beach">\n        Virginia Beach\n       </a>\n       , in the morning hours of August 27, ripping the roofs off at least five homes and damaging several others.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">\n        <a href="#cite_note-185">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       High winds in\n       <a href="/wiki/Newport_News,_Virginia" title="Newport News, Virginia">\n        Newport News\n       </a>\n       knocked a tree into an apartment complex.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6VA_186-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6VA-186">\n         [185]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">\n        <a href="#cite_note-187">\n         [186]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Three other Virginians in\n       <a href="/wiki/Brunswick_County,_Virginia" title="Brunswick County, Virginia">\n        Brunswick\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesterfield_County,_Virginia" title="Chesterfield County, Virginia">\n        Chesterfield\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/King_William_County,_Virginia" title="King William County, Virginia">\n        King William\n       </a>\n       Counties were also killed by falling trees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most severe damage consists of many downed trees on power lines, cars, homes, and roads; and flooding in many low-lying roads and neighborhoods \xe2\x80\x93 1.2 million homes and businesses lost power due to Irene.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">\n        <a href="#cite_note-188">\n         [187]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mid-Atlantic_states">\n        Mid-Atlantic states\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Mid-Atlantic states">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Irene caused widespread power outages in Delaware, Maryland, New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and Washington, D.C.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kywpower_189-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-kywpower-189">\n         [188]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190">\n        <a href="#cite_note-190">\n         [189]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">\n        <a href="#cite_note-191">\n         [190]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Maryland">\n        Maryland\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Maryland">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG/220px-Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG/330px-Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG/440px-Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Fallen_tree_in_Washington_D.C._after_Hurricane_Irene.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_RX_(XU30)#MHU33_.2F_MHU38_.282005.2C_2006.29" title="Lexus RX (XU30)">\n          Lexus RX450h\n         </a>\n         damaged by a fallen tree in Washington, D.C.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Dorchester General Hospital in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cambridge,_Maryland" title="Cambridge, Maryland">\n        Cambridge\n       </a>\n       was evacuated after there was wind and water damage\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">\n        <a href="#cite_note-192">\n         [191]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       to the laboratory roof.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193">\n        <a href="#cite_note-193">\n         [192]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Queen_Anne%27s_County,_Maryland" title="Queen Anne\'s County, Maryland">\n        Queen Anne\'s County, Maryland\n       </a>\n       , an 85-year-old woman was killed when a tree fell onto her house causing the chimney to collapse.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194">\n        <a href="#cite_note-194">\n         [193]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Farm fields on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Maryland" title="Eastern Shore of Maryland">\n        Eastern Shore of Maryland\n       </a>\n       were saturated with water after the storm, causing farmers to hand-pick their crops. Some tomato, corn, and cantaloupe crops were destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195">\n        <a href="#cite_note-195">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Delaware">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Two 25-year-old men were killed in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hockessin,_Delaware" title="Hockessin, Delaware">\n        Hockessin\n       </a>\n       area in an apparent drowning after attempting to run home through the storm on Saturday night. Their bodies were recovered near\n       <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Delaware" title="Wilmington, Delaware">\n        Wilmington\n       </a>\n       on Monday afternoon.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">\n        <a href="#cite_note-196">\n         [195]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An EF1 tornado touched down in\n       <a href="/wiki/Lewes,_Delaware" title="Lewes, Delaware">\n        Lewes\n       </a>\n       , at 6:38\xc2\xa0pm, causing a path of destruction 80 yards wide and 3/4 of a mile long, damaging about 50 homes and destroying one.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">\n        <a href="#cite_note-197">\n         [196]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Heavy rains throughout the state were topped at 10.43 inches (265\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ellendale,_Delaware" title="Ellendale, Delaware">\n        Ellendale\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198">\n         [197]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding occurred in many areas including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Bay" title="Delaware Bay">\n        Delaware Bay\n       </a>\n       communities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Slaughter_Beach,_Delaware" title="Slaughter Beach, Delaware">\n        Slaughter Beach\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Primehook_Beach,_Delaware" title="Primehook Beach, Delaware">\n        Primehook Beach\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Broadkill_Beach,_Delaware" title="Broadkill Beach, Delaware">\n        Broadkill Beach\n       </a>\n       . Sections of Prime Hook Road leading to Primehook Beach were washed out. Irene flooded and forced the closure of\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Route_1" title="Delaware Route 1">\n        Delaware Route 1\n       </a>\n       near the\n       <a href="/wiki/Indian_River_Inlet_Bridge" title="Indian River Inlet Bridge">\n        Indian River Inlet Bridge\n       </a>\n       , pushing sand onto the road.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">\n        <a href="#cite_note-199">\n         [198]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Pennsylvania">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3072" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_downed_branch_Kutztown_PA.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A downed tree branch in\n         <a href="/wiki/Kutztown,_Pennsylvania" title="Kutztown, Pennsylvania">\n          Kutztown, Pennsylvania\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Five people were killed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       : three died as a result of fallen trees, one was killed in a traffic accident, and a woman was swept away by flooding in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Wissahickon_Creek" title="Wissahickon Creek">\n        Wissahickon Creek\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       , the storm left thousands without power. More than 400 trees fell in Philadelphia, and 200 trees fell in Pittsburgh, seven buildings collapsed and twenty roads were closed.\n       <a href="/wiki/PECO_Energy_Company" title="PECO Energy Company">\n        PECO\n       </a>\n       worked on restoring power by mid-week.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">\n        <a href="#cite_note-200">\n         [199]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: New Jersey">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Irene_in_New_Jersey" title="Effects of Hurricane Irene in New Jersey">\n        Effects of Hurricane Irene in New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Raritan_River_Flood,_New_Brunswick,_NJ.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG/220px-Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG/330px-Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG/440px-Raritan_River_Flood%2C_New_Brunswick%2C_NJ.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Raritan_River_Flood,_New_Brunswick,_NJ.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The Raritan River at New Brunswick on August\xc2\xa029, 2011, one day after Hurricane Irene landfall\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       While the storm made landfall next to\n       <a href="/wiki/Galloway_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Galloway Township, New Jersey">\n        Galloway\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Little_Egg_Harbor_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Little Egg Harbor Township, New Jersey">\n        Little Egg Harbor\n       </a>\n       in the southeastern part of the state,\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Jersey" title="South Jersey">\n        South Jersey\n       </a>\n       received little damage and flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201">\n        <a href="#cite_note-201">\n         [200]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Further north, severe river flooding occurred\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202">\n        <a href="#cite_note-202">\n         [201]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       due to record rainfall,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203">\n        <a href="#cite_note-203">\n         [202]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with a statewide rainfall maxima of 11.27 inches (286\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Freehold_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Freehold Township, New Jersey">\n        Freehold\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204">\n        <a href="#cite_note-204">\n         [203]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Eleven rivers reached record levels, and a week after the storm all rivers in the state remained at "moderate flooding level".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mudflood_205-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mudflood-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The flooding affected roads, including the heavily used\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_287#Morris_County" title="Interstate 287">\n        Interstate 287\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Garden_State_Parkway" title="Garden State Parkway">\n        Garden State Parkway\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206">\n        <a href="#cite_note-206">\n         [205]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Along the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       , floodwaters affected parts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_New_Jersey" title="Jersey City, New Jersey">\n        Jersey City\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-207">\n        <a href="#cite_note-207">\n         [206]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hoboken,_New_Jersey" title="Hoboken, New Jersey">\n        Hoboken\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208">\n        <a href="#cite_note-208">\n         [207]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The north tube of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Holland_Tunnel" title="Holland Tunnel">\n        Holland Tunnel\n       </a>\n       was briefly closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-holland_209-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-holland-209">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding affected the train lines in the Trenton area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-210">\n        <a href="#cite_note-210">\n         [209]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211">\n        <a href="#cite_note-211">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm killed seven people in the state,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and damage was estimated at around $1\xc2\xa0billion.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212">\n        <a href="#cite_note-212">\n         [211]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In addition to major flooding, the combination of already heavily saturated ground from a wet summer, and heavy wind gusts made New Jersey especially vulnerable to wind damage, notably in\n       <a href="/wiki/Union_County,_New_Jersey" title="Union County, New Jersey">\n        Union County\n       </a>\n       . Fallen trees blocked vital roads, including portions of\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Route_28" title="New Jersey Route 28">\n        New Jersey Route 28\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_22" title="U.S. Route 22">\n        U.S. Route 22\n       </a>\n       . Numerous homes suffered structural damages from the wind.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2011)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       In total, approximately 1.46 million customers of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JCP%26L" title="JCP&amp;L">\n        JCP&amp;L\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Public_Service_Enterprise_Group" title="Public Service Enterprise Group">\n        PSEG\n       </a>\n       throughout most of the 21 counties lost power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-powercompany_213-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-powercompany-213">\n         [212]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On Sunday September 5, power had been returned to last remaining 2,000 residents who suffered a\n       <a href="/wiki/Power_outage" title="Power outage">\n        power outage\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214">\n        <a href="#cite_note-214">\n         [213]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Flooding in some parts of the state continued for another three days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215">\n        <a href="#cite_note-215">\n         [214]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216">\n        <a href="#cite_note-216">\n         [215]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 31,\n       <a href="/wiki/Paterson,_New_Jersey" title="Paterson, New Jersey">\n        Paterson\n       </a>\n       counted 6,000 displaced persons, and three of four bridges crossing the\n       <a href="/wiki/Passaic_River" title="Passaic River">\n        Passaic River\n       </a>\n       remained closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217">\n        <a href="#cite_note-217">\n         [216]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August\xc2\xa031, President\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        Barack Obama\n       </a>\n       declared the state a\n       <a href="/wiki/Disaster_area" title="Disaster area">\n        disaster area\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disaster_area_218-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-disaster_area-218">\n         [217]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       including all\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_counties_in_New_Jersey" title="List of counties in New Jersey">\n        21 counties\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219">\n        <a href="#cite_note-219">\n         [218]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 31,000 residents filed assistance claims through FEMA, and within two weeks nearly $38 million had been disbursed with others pending. Hardest-hit counties were\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bergen_County" title="Bergen County">\n        Bergen\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Passaic_County" title="Passaic County">\n        Passaic\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gateway_Region" title="Gateway Region">\n        northeast\n       </a>\n       , each with more than 4,000 claims.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220">\n        <a href="#cite_note-220">\n         [219]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Despite the mandatory evacuations ordered for many parts of the Jersey Shore, the damage and flooding in that area of the state was not as severe as predicted. This miscalculation was met with frustration among many coastal residents that were evacuated out of an abundance of caution. A year later when evacuations were ordered for Hurricane Sandy, some residents were reluctant or skeptical about the storm\'s potential and their preparations were more lax. This proved very damaging for some as Hurricane Sandy was far worse than predicted.\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_York">\n        New York\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: New York">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Irene_in_New_York" title="Effects of Hurricane Irene in New York">\n        Effects of Hurricane Irene in New York\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Manhattan" title="Manhattan">\n        Manhattan\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       flooded in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Meatpacking_District" title="Meatpacking District">\n        Meatpacking District\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-holland_209-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-holland-209">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Beach,_New_York" title="Long Beach, New York">\n        Long Beach\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Freeport,_New_York" title="Freeport, New York">\n        Freeport\n       </a>\n       , both of which experienced serious flooding, were among the worst-hit towns on Long Island,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Long_Island_221-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Long_Island-221">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and many roads were left impassable. The workers at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ground_Zero" title="Ground Zero">\n        Ground Zero\n       </a>\n       in Lower Manhattan worked to make the World Trade Center site hurricane proof, and escaped major damage, just missing the tenth anniversary of 9/11.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Long_Island_221-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Long_Island-221">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The winds knocked down many trees and power lines, leaving almost 350,000 homes and businesses without power in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nassau_County,_New_York" title="Nassau County, New York">\n        Nassau\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Suffolk_County,_New_York" title="Suffolk County, New York">\n        Suffolk\n       </a>\n       counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222">\n        <a href="#cite_note-222">\n         [221]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ramapo_River" title="Ramapo River">\n        Ramapo River\n       </a>\n       and more than a half-mile (1\xc2\xa0km) of washouts led both Metro-North and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Transit_Rail_Operations" title="New Jersey Transit Rail Operations">\n        NJ Transit\n       </a>\n       to suspend service on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Jervis_Line" title="Port Jervis Line">\n        Port Jervis Line\n       </a>\n       north of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suffern_(NJT_station)" title="Suffern (NJT station)">\n        Suffern\n       </a>\n       for nearly three months.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Port_Jervis_Line_suspension_223-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Port_Jervis_Line_suspension-223">\n         [222]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224">\n        <a href="#cite_note-224">\n         [223]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding overwhelmed several\n       <a href="/wiki/Sewage_treatment" title="Sewage treatment">\n        sewage treatment\n       </a>\n       plants, since many of them collect and processed storm\n       <a href="/wiki/Surface_runoff" title="Surface runoff">\n        runoff\n       </a>\n       as well as\n       <a href="/wiki/Wastewater" title="Wastewater">\n        wastewater\n       </a>\n       . At least 52 municipalities in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_Valley" title="Hudson Valley">\n        Hudson Valley\n       </a>\n       reported raw-sewage spills into local waters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_sewage_failures_story_225-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_sewage_failures_story-225">\n         [224]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Vaccinations against\n       <a href="/wiki/Tetanus" title="Tetanus">\n        tetanus\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hepatitis" title="Hepatitis">\n        hepatitis\n       </a>\n       were offered to rescuers before entering houses in some areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_Goshen_sewage_story_226-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_Goshen_sewage_story-226">\n         [225]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Parts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Washingtonville,_New_York" title="Washingtonville, New York">\n        Washingtonville\n       </a>\n       were under 8 feet (2.4\xc2\xa0m) of water during the storm due to the flash flood of\n       <a href="/wiki/Moodna_Creek" title="Moodna Creek">\n        Moodna Creek\n       </a>\n       , wrecking some nearby homes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_Washingtonville_story_227-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_Washingtonville_story-227">\n         [226]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Disastrous flash floods occurred in the northwestern\n       <a href="/wiki/Catskill_Mountains" title="Catskill Mountains">\n        Catskill Mountains\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228">\n        <a href="#cite_note-228">\n         [227]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Record flooding along the\n       <a href="/wiki/Schoharie_Creek" title="Schoharie Creek">\n        Schoharie Creek\n       </a>\n       destroyed the 156-year-old\n       <a href="/wiki/Old_Blenheim_Bridge" title="Old Blenheim Bridge">\n        Old Blenheim Bridge\n       </a>\n       , a\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Historic_Landmark" title="National Historic Landmark">\n        National Historic Landmark\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229">\n        <a href="#cite_note-229">\n         [228]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Local officials estimated that approximately one-third of all the houses and businesses in the village of Schoharie had been destroyed due to flooding. The Gilboa Dam, built in 1926, which had undergone some strengthening procedures during 2005 and 2006, sustained minor damage due to the flooding of the Schoharie Creek. Further upstate, Irene did significant damage in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Adirondack_Mountains" title="Adirondack Mountains">\n        Adirondack Mountains\n       </a>\n       . A section of\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_State_Route_73" title="New York State Route 73">\n        NY 73\n       </a>\n       was washed out, isolating two hamlets.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Keene_story_230-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Keene_story-230">\n         [229]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       DEC reported that "\n       <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">\n        landslides\n       </a>\n       too numerous to count" had taken place on many of the High Peaks themselves, all of which are located on state\n       <a href="/wiki/Forest_Preserve_(New_York)" title="Forest Preserve (New York)">\n        Forest Preserve\n       </a>\n       land.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DEC_ADK_closures_231-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-DEC_ADK_closures-231">\n         [230]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall, there were ten deaths in the state, most due to flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcr_3-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcr-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On September 3, Governor Cuomo announced the creation of a $15 million federal relief fund to help farmers there cope with the damage,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Saturday_power_story_232-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Saturday_power_story-232">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       after an estimated $45 million in crop damage on 145,000 acres (59,000\xc2\xa0ha).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_farmers_story_233-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_farmers_story-233">\n         [232]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In mid-September, farmers reported a smaller-than-average harvest of pumpkins in the northeastern United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pumpkinshortage_234-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-pumpkinshortage-234">\n         [233]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Many farmers in the Black Dirt Region were near bankruptcy by that point, and fundraisers were being held to tide them over pending federal disaster relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Warwick_Farm_Aid_235-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Warwick_Farm_Aid-235">\n         [234]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Farmers were worried the reports would deter tourists from\n       <a href="/wiki/Agritourism#Agritourism_in_the_United_States" title="Agritourism">\n        visiting farm country\n       </a>\n       for traditional autumn activities and purchases, an economic setback which some said would exacerbate the damage from the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_September_farm_damage_story_236-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_September_farm_damage_story-236">\n         [235]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Many planned to remain open and offer what they could to visitors.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-THR_agritourism_story_237-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-THR_agritourism_story-237">\n         [236]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 226.66666666667px">\n        <div style="width: 226.66666666667px">\n <div style="width: 202px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 200px;">\n          <div style="margin:0px auto;">\n           <a class="image" 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Forge_Hill_Road_bridge_washout_after_Hurricane_Irene%2C_New_Windsor%2C_NY.jpg/600px-Forge_Hill_Road_bridge_washout_after_Hurricane_Irene%2C_New_Windsor%2C_NY.jpg title="New Windsor, New York">\n            New Windsor\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_England_2">\n        New England\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: New England">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Connecticut">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich,_CT.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1936" data-file-width="2592" height="164" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG/220px-Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG/330px-Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG/440px-Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich%2C_CT.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_Storm_Surge_in_Greenwich,_CT.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n          Storm surge\n         </a>\n         from Hurricane Irene in\n         <a href="/wiki/Greenwich,_Connecticut" title="Greenwich, Connecticut">\n          Greenwich, Connecticut\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       , 20 homes in\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Haven,_Connecticut" title="East Haven, Connecticut">\n        East Haven\n       </a>\n       were destroyed and five others were damaged beyond repair by flooding and storm surge along the shore of\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Island_Sound" title="Long Island Sound">\n        Long Island Sound\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CT_238-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CT-238">\n         [237]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On Sunday, Connecticut\'s two main electric companies, Connecticut Light and Power and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Illuminating" title="United Illuminating">\n        United Illuminating\n       </a>\n       , reported that a record 754,000 customers, about half the state, were without power. More than two days after the storm made landfall, about 400,000 people were still without power, some being told they would have to wait more than a week, especially in heavily wooded areas. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Ridgefield,_Connecticut" title="Ridgefield, Connecticut">\n        Ridgefield\n       </a>\n       , 90% of houses lost power, requiring the utility to turn off power to the other 10% to ease restoration efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-239">\n        <a href="#cite_note-239">\n         [238]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240">\n        <a href="#cite_note-240">\n         [239]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut_Route_15" title="Connecticut Route 15">\n        Route 15\n       </a>\n       , one of the state\'s main highways, was closed from the New York state line to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Interstate_91_in_Connecticut" title="Interstate 91 in Connecticut">\n        Interstate 91\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Meriden,_Connecticut" title="Meriden, Connecticut">\n        Meriden\n       </a>\n       due to fallen trees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-241">\n        <a href="#cite_note-241">\n         [240]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Dannel_Malloy" title="Dannel Malloy">\n        Dannel Malloy\n       </a>\n       said Hurricane Irene was responsible for a tenth death on August 28: a man who died in a fire likely caused by downed wires from high winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242">\n        <a href="#cite_note-242">\n         [241]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An elderly woman, who resided in\n       <a href="/wiki/Prospect,_Connecticut" title="Prospect, Connecticut">\n        Prospect\n       </a>\n       , died in similar situations, when a falling tree caused power lines to collapse onto her home, starting a fire;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       her husband was critically injured.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-243">\n        <a href="#cite_note-243">\n         [242]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Bristol,_Connecticut" title="Bristol, Connecticut">\n        Bristol\n       </a>\n       , a man drowned when his canoe capsized.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A week later, many homes in Connecticut still had not had their power restored.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Connecticut_Light_%26_Power" title="Connecticut Light &amp; Power">\n        Connecticut Light &amp; Power\n       </a>\n       said on September 2 that it was ahead of where it expected to be, and that less than 100,000 customers would still be without power by midnight the next day. Crews had come from many distant places in North America, including\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Columbia" title="British Columbia">\n        British Columbia\n       </a>\n       , to help the utility\'s own crews.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Saturday_power_story_232-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Saturday_power_story-232">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The continued outages also meant that in rural areas with private wells, residents still lacked running water a week after the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_CT_water_story_244-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_CT_water_story-244">\n         [243]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Massachusetts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       , damage was greatest in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Western_Massachusetts#The_Hill_Towns" title="Western Massachusetts">\n        Hill Towns\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Western_Massachusetts" title="Western Massachusetts">\n        Western Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       as the eye of the storm tracked westward, toward Albany, New York.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2011)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       High winds toppled trees and heavy rain caused widespread flooding of Connecticut River tributaries. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Westfield_River" title="Westfield River">\n        Westfield River\n       </a>\n       rose almost twenty feet in a matter of hours; the\n       <a href="/wiki/Deerfield_River" title="Deerfield River">\n        Deerfield River\n       </a>\n       rose over fifteen feet in the same period. Both rivers reached flood stages not seen since the 1955, and 1938, hurricanes and floods.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-245">\n        <a href="#cite_note-245">\n         [244]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A 6-mile stretch of\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_Route_2" title="Massachusetts Route 2">\n        Route 2\n       </a>\n       from Charlemont to Florida along the Cold River branch of the Deerfield was closed due to damage for over 3 months.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-246">\n        <a href="#cite_note-246">\n         [245]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A\n       <a href="/wiki/Public_works" title="Public works">\n        public works\n       </a>\n       employee was electrocuted by downed power lines in\n       <a href="/wiki/Southbridge,_Massachusetts" title="Southbridge, Massachusetts">\n        Southbridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A dam failure was mistakenly reported in\n       <a href="/wiki/Becket,_Massachusetts" title="Becket, Massachusetts">\n        East Becket\n       </a>\n       , yet 200 people were evacuated as a precaution.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-247">\n        <a href="#cite_note-247">\n         [246]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 227.33333333333px">\n        <div style="width: 227.33333333333px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 225.33333333333px;">\n          <div style="margin:0px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="697" data-file-width="1045" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg/338px-Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg/507px-Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg/675px-Hurricane_Irene_-_Lynn_Beach.jpg 2x" width="226"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Sailboats broke from their moorings and washed ashore in Massachusetts\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 202px">\n        <div style="width: 202px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 200px;">\n          <div style="margin:0px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg/300px-Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg/451px-Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg/600px-Irene_Two_Broken_Trees.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Two trees toppled by Irene in coastal Massachusetts.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rhode_Island">\n        Rhode Island\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Rhode Island">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rhode_Island" title="Rhode Island">\n        Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       had gusts of wind up to 71\xc2\xa0mph (114\xc2\xa0km/h),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-248">\n        <a href="#cite_note-248">\n         [247]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       uprooting trees and causing extensive damage to its power grid. By the storm\'s end, an estimated 256,000 out of 480,281 customers were without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-249">\n        <a href="#cite_note-249">\n         [248]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rhode Island electric company,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Grid_USA" title="National Grid USA">\n        National Grid\n       </a>\n       , expected it to take until Labor Day weekend to restore power to the most remote areas and areas which were most damaged. On August 30, two days after the storm, 138,000 customers remained without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-250">\n        <a href="#cite_note-250">\n         [249]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A power line on\n       <a href="/wiki/Aquidneck_Island" title="Aquidneck Island">\n        Aquidneck Island\n       </a>\n       near\n       <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth,_Rhode_Island" title="Portsmouth, Rhode Island">\n        Portsmouth\n       </a>\n       was felled by winds during the morning of August 28, severing power to Portsmouth,\n       <a href="/wiki/Middletown,_Rhode_Island" title="Middletown, Rhode Island">\n        Middletown\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Newport,_Rhode_Island" title="Newport, Rhode Island">\n        Newport\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Jamestown,_Rhode_Island" title="Jamestown, Rhode Island">\n        Jamestown\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-251">\n        <a href="#cite_note-251">\n         [250]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Power was not fully restored to Aquidneck Island and\n       <a href="/wiki/Conanicut_Island" title="Conanicut Island">\n        Conanicut Island\n       </a>\n       communities until August 30. The storm surge into Narragansett Bay caused some coastal damage, although\n       <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">\n        Providence\n       </a>\n       , at the head of the bay, was spared downtown flooding in part due to its\n       <a href="/wiki/Fox_Point_Hurricane_Barrier" title="Fox Point Hurricane Barrier">\n        hurricane barrier\n       </a>\n       . There was some localized river flooding,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-252">\n        <a href="#cite_note-252">\n         [251]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       however being on the eastern side of the storm, most of the damage came in the form of wind.\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Vermont">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Almost every river and stream in\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">\n        Vermont\n       </a>\n       flooded, resulting in at least three deaths and one missing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC6_165-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC6-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-253">\n        <a href="#cite_note-253">\n         [252]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-254">\n        <a href="#cite_note-254">\n         [253]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_Vermont" title="Wilmington, Vermont">\n        Wilmington\n       </a>\n       , the flood level of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Deerfield_River" title="Deerfield River">\n        Deerfield River\n       </a>\n       east branch reportedly exceeded levels measured during the\n       <a href="/wiki/1938_New_England_hurricane" title="1938 New England hurricane">\n        1938 New England hurricane\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x93 the only other tropical cyclone to make a direct hit on Vermont in the state\'s recorded history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-255">\n        <a href="#cite_note-255">\n         [254]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Throughout Vermont, numerous\n       <a href="/wiki/Covered_bridge" title="Covered bridge">\n        covered bridges\n       </a>\n       , many over 100 years old, were damaged or destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-256">\n        <a href="#cite_note-256">\n         [255]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Extensive road damage resulted in the isolation of over a dozen rural towns that would require helicopter air-lifts of necessities in the days immediately following the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-257">\n        <a href="#cite_note-257">\n         [256]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm decimated multiple sections of\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_4" title="U.S. Route 4">\n        U.S. Route 4\n       </a>\n       between\n       <a href="/wiki/Rutland_(city),_Vermont" title="Rutland (city), Vermont">\n        Rutland\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quechee,_VT" title="Quechee, VT">\n        Quechee\n       </a>\n       , making east/west travel through the southern part of state nearly impossible. The resort town of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Killington,_VT" title="Killington, VT">\n        Killington\n       </a>\n       as well as neighboring\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pittsfield,_VT" title="Pittsfield, VT">\n        Pittsfield\n       </a>\n       were completely isolated from travel in and out for two weeks. Statewide, the cost of repairs for road and bridge damage alone was estimated to exceed $700 million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-258">\n        <a href="#cite_note-258">\n         [257]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Relief concerts were organized by local Vermont bands such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Phish" title="Phish">\n        Phish\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-259">\n        <a href="#cite_note-259">\n         [258]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Grace_Potter_and_the_Nocturnals" title="Grace Potter and the Nocturnals">\n        Grace Potter and the Nocturnals\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-260">\n        <a href="#cite_note-260">\n         [259]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By December the state was recovering more quickly than originally expected. Within a month of the storm 84 of 118 closed sections of state highway, and 28 of 34 bridges, had been reopened. The state had relied on assistance from\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Guard_of_the_United_States" title="National Guard of the United States">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       units in eight other states, and highway workers lent to it by New Hampshire and Maine. "We\'ll do the work and we\'ll figure out how we\'re paying for it," said deputy state secretary of transportation\n       <a href="/wiki/Sue_Minter" title="Sue Minter">\n        Sue Minter\n       </a>\n       , "but we\'re not waiting." Repair costs ultimately turned out to be $175\xe2\x80\x93200 million, with most of it covered by federal disaster relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Vermont_Irene_recovery_article_261-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Vermont_Irene_recovery_article-261">\n         [260]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 152px">\n        <div style="width: 152px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div Taftsville bridge.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 378px">\n        <div style="width: 378px">\n         <div class="thumb" Royalton, Vermont bridge.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Maine">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Tropical storm conditions occurred throughout the state of Maine during Irene\'s passage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-262">\n        <a href="#cite_note-262">\n         [261]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding caused by Irene\'s heavy rainfall washed out two bridges on\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine_State_Route_27" title="Maine State Route 27">\n        State Route 27\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Carrabassett_Valley,_Maine" title="Carrabassett Valley, Maine">\n        Carrabassett Valley\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-263">\n        <a href="#cite_note-263">\n         [262]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Canada_2">\n        Canada\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Canada">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Irene also affected a large section of Canada, stretching from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Ontario" title="Eastern Ontario">\n        eastern\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Ontario" title="Ontario">\n        Ontario\n       </a>\n       to the coasts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Newfoundland and Labrador">\n        Newfoundland and Labrador\n       </a>\n       . On August 28, in\n       <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">\n        Quebec\n       </a>\n       , high winds (more than 110 kilometres per hour (68\xc2\xa0mph) in some places) and heavy rainfall from post-tropical storm Irene knocked out power to over 250,000 homes, felled tree branches, and damaged buildings and traffic signals across\n       <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">\n        Montreal\n       </a>\n       . One person was killed after a road was washed out and cars were swept into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yamaska_River" title="Yamaska River">\n        Yamaska River\n       </a>\n       near\n       <a href="/wiki/Sorel-Tracy" title="Sorel-Tracy">\n        Sorel-Tracy\n       </a>\n       ; another section of road in\n       <a href="/wiki/Charlevoix" title="Charlevoix">\n        Charlevoix\n       </a>\n       was also washed out, while flooding forced evacuations in\n       <a href="/wiki/Estrie" title="Estrie">\n        Estrie\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-264">\n        <a href="#cite_note-264">\n         [263]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-265">\n        <a href="#cite_note-265">\n         [264]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-266">\n        <a href="#cite_note-266">\n         [265]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick" title="New Brunswick">\n        New Brunswick\n       </a>\n       , many trees fell in the wake of the hurricane, mainly due to the strong winds associated with the storm. Power was lost to an estimated 75,000 \xe2\x80\x93 200,000 New Brunswick residents, directly due to the gale-force winds. Insured damage in Canada was estimated at $130 million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ibcdamage_112-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ibcdamage-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Retirement">\n        Retirement\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Retirement">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Atlantic_hurricane_names" title="List of retired Atlantic hurricane names">\n        List of retired Atlantic hurricane names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Because of the extreme damage and deaths caused by the storm, the name\n       <i>\n        Irene\n       </i>\n       was later retired by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       (WMO), and won\'t be used again for an\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_hurricane" title="Atlantic hurricane">\n        Atlantic tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       . It was replaced with\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n         Irma\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       for the\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2017 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-267">\n        <a href="#cite_note-267">\n         [266]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Irene&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit
